2004-02-23: judgej@acad-ajp.: ChangeSet 1.1766.52.6
  Bug 2318: extend validation of block state to include '0'=='hidden'A few other bugs that came to light are also fixed in this patch:- 'delete' JS message switched from optional 'title' (which may be blank)to 'name'.- 'delete' JS message now properly escaped to prevent JS errors that wereoccuring when quotes appeared in the delete message.- 'delete' JS message translated in the script before being passed to the template. This allows a proper translation using #(1) fields - somethingthat is simply not possible in a template as no '#' may appear between a pair of '#'s in a tag attribute. An earlier bug raised on this is set'WONTFIX', so this alternative method of preparing the text in the GUIscript is necessary.

  Bug 1864: 'back' button removed from exception templates (all four).It was misleading, and implied that users could go back and re-entertheir previous form, which they could not due to the way the authorisationkey works.Perhaps - just perhaps - the authorisation key could be *checked* at thestart of a GUI handler, and then *consumed* only after all other validationhas passed? That would allow the 'back' link to be put back in. I don'tknow what the risks would be though.
